   $(document).ready(function () {
                //check for gaq
                if (typeof _gaq != 'undefined') {
                    // Track shirt clicks
                    $('.kit-content-league').on('click', 'ul li a', function (e) {
                        e.preventDefault();
                        var team = $(this).attr('title'),
                                url = $(this).attr('href');
                        if (typeof team != 'undefined') {
                            _gaq.push([
                                '_trackEvent',
                                'Shirts Nav',
                                'Click',
                                team
                            ]);
                            _gaq.push(function () {
                                window.location.href = url;
                            });
                        }
                    });
                    //Track League changes
                    $('.kit-nav-dropdown-button select').change(function () {
                        var league = $('.kit-nav-dropdown-button select :selected').text().trim();
                        _gaq.push([
                            '_trackEvent',
                            'Shirts Nav',
                            'Change',
                            league
                        ]);
                    });
                }
            });
  </script>

	function showGoalsConcededGraph(argType){
		 for(var i=0; i<parseInt(arr_goals_conceded_types.length); i++){
		 	if(arr_goals_conceded_types[i] == argType)
		 		jq('#the-graph-3-'+arr_goals_conceded_types[i]).show();
		 	else
		 		jq('#the-graph-3-'+arr_goals_conceded_types[i]).hide();
		 }
		 squawkaDp.drawGoalsConceded(argType);
	}

	function showDuelsWon(val){
		if(parseInt(val) > 0){
			jq("#duel_won_suc").show();
			jq("#duel_won_fail").hide();
		}
		else{
			jq("#duel_won_suc").hide();
			jq("#duel_won_fail").show();
		}
	}
	
	showDuelsWon(53);

	{

		}
		else
		{
			jq('#stat-graph-9-passlength').show();
			jq('#stat-graph-9-overtime').hide();
		}

		averagePassLength(type);
	}

    function performanceScoreChart(datas) {
		// Create and populate the data table.
		// Attacking - Attacking Performance Score over game dates
		// Possesive - Possesive Performance Score over game dates
		// Defensive - Defensive Performance Score over game dates
		// Overall - Overall Performance Score over game dates
		if(arguments.length == 2)
		{
			if(arguments[1] == 'ot')
			 {
			 	jq('#perform_over_time').show();
			 	jq('#perform_cumulative').hide();
			 }
			else
			{
				jq('#perform_cumulative').show();
			 	jq('#perform_over_time').hide();
			}
		}
		else
		{
			jq('#perform_over_time').show();
			jq('#perform_cumulative').hide();
		}

		if(arguments[1] == 'ot' || arguments.length==1){
			var data = google.visualization.arrayToDataTable(datas);
	
			// Create and draw the visualization.
			new google.visualization.LineChart(document.getElementById('the-graph-1')).
				draw(data, {curveType: "function",
							width: 557, height: 280,
							vAxis: {maxValue: 10}, legend : {position: 'top'}, pointSize:5
							}
					);
		}
		
		if(arguments[1] == 'cumulative'){
			var x		=	new Array('x', 'Attacking', 'Possession', 'Defensive', 'Overall');
			var ot_data	=	new Array();
			ot_data.push(x);
			ot_data.push(new Array(datas[1][0], datas[1][1], datas[1][2], datas[1][3], datas[1][4]));			
			for(i=2;i<datas.length;i++)
			{
				var y	=	new Array();
				y.push(datas[i][0]);
				y.push(Number(parseFloat(datas[i][1] + ot_data[i-1][1]).toFixed(2)));
				y.push(Number(parseFloat(datas[i][2] + ot_data[i-1][2]).toFixed(2)));
				y.push(Number(parseFloat(datas[i][3] + ot_data[i-1][3]).toFixed(2)));
				y.push(Number(parseFloat(datas[i][4] + ot_data[i-1][4]).toFixed(2)));
				ot_data.push(y);			
			}
			
			
			//console.log(ot_data);
			var data = google.visualization.arrayToDataTable(ot_data);
			new google.visualization.LineChart(document.getElementById('the-graph-1ot')).
					draw(data, {curveType: "function",
								width: 537, height: 280,
								vAxis: {maxValue: 10},
								pointSize:5
								}
						);
		}
	}
	
	function goalsPerMatch(dates,others) {
		others = eval(others);
		
		// Some raw data (not necessarily accurate)
		var data = google.visualization.arrayToDataTable(dates);
	  
		// Create and draw the visualization.
		var ac = new google.visualization.AreaChart(document.getElementById('the-graph-3'));
		ac.draw(data, {
		  isStacked: true,
		  width: 557,
		  height: 280,
		  vAxis: {title: "Cumulative Goals Scored"},
		  hAxis: {title: "Game Date"}
		});
		
		// Create and populate the data table.
		  var data = google.visualization.arrayToDataTable([
			['Body part Type', 'Resulting Goals'],
			['Headed', others.headed],
			['Left foot', others.leftfoot],
			['Right foot', others.rightfoot],
			['Other', others.bodypartother]
		  ]);
		
		  // Create and draw the visualization.
			new google.visualization.PieChart(document.getElementById('the-graph-3a')).
				draw(data, {
					width: 557,
		  			height: 280
				});
				
		// Create and populate the data table.
		  var data = google.visualization.arrayToDataTable([
			['Set Piece Type', 'Resulting Goals'],
			['Crossed Free Kicks', others.crossedfreekick],
			['Direct Free Kicks', others.directfreekick],
			['Corners', others.corner],
			['Throw Ins', others.throwin],
			['Penalties', others.penalty],
			['Other',others.typeother]
		  ]);
		
		  // Create and draw the visualization.
			new google.visualization.PieChart(document.getElementById('the-graph-3b')).
				draw(data, {
					width: 557,
		  			height: 280
				});
		
	  }

				/** End */
			}	
			
		}
				
		
		function averagePossesion() {
		  var datas  = eval(global_average_possession);
		  var MARKER = '$^$';
		  // Create and populate the data table.
		  var data = google.visualization.arrayToDataTable(datas);
			
		  var formatter = new google.visualization.NumberFormat({suffix: '%',fractionDigits: 0});
		  formatter.format(data,1);
		  formatter.format(data,2);
		
		  // Create and draw the visualization.
		  new google.visualization.ComboChart(document.getElementById('the-graph-7')).
			  draw(data, {curveType: "function",
					width: 557, height: 280,
					vAxis: {
						viewWindowMode:'explicit',
		              	viewWindow:{
		                	max:85,
		                	min:25
		              	},
		              	format:MARKER + '#'
					},
					seriesType: "bars",
          			series: {1: {type: "line", lineWidth: 2, visibleInLegend: true}},
          			legend:"none"
					});
					
			jq("text:contains('" + MARKER + "')").each(
					function(label, index) {
						val = jq(this).text().replace(MARKER, '');
						jq(this).text(val+'%');
				});	
		}
		
		function passAccuracy(argType) {
			
			var scales = eval(obj_pass_accuracy);
			
			if(argType == 'accuracy'){
			  // Create and populate the data table.
			  var data = google.visualization.arrayToDataTable([
				['Pass Accuracy', 'General', 'Headed', 'Through Ball', 'Cross', 'Long Ball'],
				['Successful Passes ', scales.successfull['other'], scales.successfull['headed_pass'], scales.successfull['through_ball'], scales.successfull['cross'], scales.successfull['long_ball']],
				['Unsuccessful Passes ', scales.unsuccessfull['other'], scales.unsuccessfull['headed_pass'], scales.unsuccessfull['through_ball'], scales.unsuccessfull['cross'], scales.unsuccessfull['long_ball']]
			  ]);
			
			  // Create and draw the visualization.
			  new google.visualization.ColumnChart(document.getElementById('the-graph-8')).
				  draw(data,
					   {isStacked: true,
						width:557, height:280} //,vAxis: {maxValue: 100}
				  );
			}
		  
			if(argType == 'type'){
				// Create and populate the data table.
			  var data = google.visualization.arrayToDataTable([
				['Pass Type', 'Resulting Passes'],
				['Forward', scales.forward],
				['Backward', scales.backward]
			  ]);
			
			  // Create and draw the visualization.
				new google.visualization.PieChart(document.getElementById('the-graph-8a')).
					draw(data, {
						width: 557,
			  			height: 280
					});
			}
		}
		
		function pass_acc_dual_scale()
		{ 
			var MARKER = '$^$';
			var datas = eval(global_pass_acc_overtime);
			var x		=	new Array('x', 'All passes', '% pass accuracy');
			var ot_data	=	new Array();
			ot_data.push(x);
			ot_data.push(new Array(datas[1][0], datas[1][1], datas[1][2]));			
			for(i=2;i<datas.length;i++)
			{
				var y	=	new Array();
				y.push(datas[i][0]);
				y.push(datas[i][1]);	// + ot_data[i-1][1]
				y.push(datas[i][2]);
				ot_data.push(y);			
			} 
			var data = google.visualization.arrayToDataTable(ot_data);
			/*var formatter = new google.visualization.NumberFormat(
			      {suffix: '%', negativeColor: 'red', negativeParens: true});
			formatter.format(data, 2);*/
			if(jq('#the-graph-8-ot').css('display') == 'none')
			  	jq('#the-graph-8-ot').css('visibility','hidden').css('display','block');
				// Create and draw the visualization.
				new google.visualization.LineChart(document.getElementById('the-graph-8ot')).
					draw(data, {curveType: "function",
								width: 537, height: 280,
								vAxis: {0: {logScale: false, maxValue: 10},
	            						1: {logScale: false, maxValue: 75, viewWindow:{max:100, min:0}, viewWindowMode :'explicit'}
	            						, format: MARKER + '#'},
								pointSize:5,
							    series:{
							       0:{targetAxisIndex:0},
							       1:{targetAxisIndex:1}},
								legend: {position: 'top'}
							       }
						);
						
				jq("text:contains('" + MARKER + "')").each(
					function(label, index) {
						//console.log(label + jq(this).text());
						val = jq(this).text().replace(MARKER, '');
						if(label > 4  )
						jq(this).text(val+'%');
						else
						jq(this).text(val);
				});		
				/** End */  
				if(jq('#the-graph-8-ot').css('visibility') == 'hidden')
			  		jq('#the-graph-8-ot').css('visibility','visible').css('display','none');
		}

		function discipline(argType) {
				
			var y_violence 	= 	global_cards[0];
			var y_tackling 	= 	global_cards[1];
			var y_verbal 	= 	global_cards[2];
			var y_other 	= 	global_cards[3];
			var r_violence 	= 	global_cards[4];
			var r_tackling 	= 	global_cards[5];
			var r_verbal 	= 	global_cards[6];
			var r_other 	= 	global_cards[7];
			
			if(argType == "yellow"){
			  	// Create and populate the data table.
			 	var data = google.visualization.arrayToDataTable([
					['Type', 			'Violence', 	'Tackling', 	'Verbal',	'Other'],
					['Yellow Cards',  	y_violence,  	y_tackling,  	y_verbal,	y_other]
			  	]);
			
			  	// Create and draw the visualization.
				var total		=	parseInt(y_violence+y_tackling+y_verbal+y_other);
				var min_val 	= 	(total >= 5)		?1:0;
				//min_val			=	0;
				var grid_val 	= 	(total >= 5)	?5:(total < 2)?2:total;
			  	new google.visualization.ColumnChart(document.getElementById('the-graph-12')).
				draw(data,
				{
					width:557, 
					height:280,
					isStacked: true,
					vAxis: {
						format:'#',
						gridlines:{
							count:grid_val
						},
			        	viewWindowMode:'explicit',
			            viewWindow:{
			            	min:min_val
			            }
		            },
		            colors:['#FFFF00','#FFD800','#F4C430','#FBEC5D']
				});	
			}
			
			if(argType == "red"){
				// Create and populate the data table.
			  	var data = google.visualization.arrayToDataTable([
					['Type', 			'Violence', 	'Tackling', 	'Verbal',	'Other'],
					['Red Cards',  		r_violence,   	r_tackling,  	r_verbal,	r_other]
			  	]);
	
				// Create and draw the visualization.
				var total		=	parseInt(r_violence+r_tackling+r_verbal+r_other);
				var min_val 	= 	(total > 5)		?1:0;
				min_val			=	0;
				var grid_val 	= 	(total >= 5)	?5:(total < 2)?2:total;
				new google.visualization.ColumnChart(document.getElementById('the-graph-12a')).
				draw(data,
				{
					width:557, 
					height:280,
					isStacked: true,
					vAxis: {
						format:'#',
						gridlines:{
							count:grid_val
						},
						viewWindowMode:'explicit',
				    	viewWindow:{
				    		min:min_val
				    	}
					},
					colors:['#FF0000','#E34234','#C41E3A','#E30B5C']
				});
			}
		}

		var shotAccuracy_total_ontargets = 89;
		var shotAccuracy_total_goals = 31;
		var shotAccuracy_total_attempts	 = 192;
		var active_hover	=	0;
		function shotAccuracyConversion()
		{
			total_ontargets = shotAccuracy_total_ontargets;
			total_goals = shotAccuracy_total_goals;
			jq("#sa_goalmouth").hide();
			jq("#sa_zone").hide();
			jq("#sa_conversion").show();
			 // Create and populate the data table.
		  var data = google.visualization.arrayToDataTable([
			['Shot Type', 'Number of Occurences'],
			['Goals',total_goals],
			['Failed', (total_ontargets-total_goals)]
		  ]);
		
		  // Create and draw the visualization.
			new google.visualization.PieChart(document.getElementById('the-graph-5a')).
				draw(data, {
					width: 557,
		  			height: 280
				});
			
		}
		
		function drawShotAccuracypercent()
		{
			jq("#the-graph-5-zone").hide();
			jq("#shotaccuracy_overtime").show();			
			jq("#sa_conversion").hide();
						
			var MARKER			=	'$^$';
			var goalscored_ot	=	shotaccuracy_overtimedata;
					var x				=	new Array('x', 'Avg Shot accuracy');
					var datas			=	new Array();
					datas.push(x);
					jq.each(goalscored_ot, function()
					{
						var y 	=	new Array();
						y.push(this.date);
						var ontarget	=	parseFloat(this.ontarget);
						var offtarget	=	parseFloat(this.offtarget);				 
						y.push(Math.round((ontarget/(ontarget+offtarget))*100));
						datas.push(y);
					});
				
			
			datas = eval(datas); 
			var data = google.visualization.arrayToDataTable(datas);
	
			// Create and draw the visualization.
			new google.visualization.LineChart(document.getElementById('the-graph-saot')).
				draw(data, {curveType: "function",
							width: 567, height: 280,
							vAxis: {maxValue: 10,
									format: MARKER+'#'}, 
							pointSize:5
							}
					);
			jq("text:contains('" + MARKER + "')").each(
					function(label, index) {
						val = jq(this).text().replace(MARKER, '');
						jq(this).text(val+'%');
				});		
		}
		
		function drawShotAccuracyOvertime(){
			
			jq("#the-graph-5-zone").hide();
			jq("#shotaccuracy_overtime").hide();
			jq("#sa_conversion").show();	
			
			var goalscored_ot	=	shotaccuracy_overtimedata;
					var x				=	new Array('x', 'Head', 'Left Foot', 'Right Foot', 'Other',	'Overall');
					var datas			=	new Array();
					datas.push(x);
					jq.each(goalscored_ot, function()
					{
						var y 	=	new Array();
						y.push(this.date);
						y.push(parseFloat(this.head));
						y.push(parseFloat(this.leftfoot));
						y.push(parseFloat(this.rightfoot));
						y.push(parseFloat(this.other));
						y.push(parseFloat(this.total));
						datas.push(y);
					});
				
			
			datas = eval(datas); 
			var data = google.visualization.arrayToDataTable(datas);
	
			// Create and draw the visualization.
			new google.visualization.LineChart(document.getElementById('the-graph-5a')).
				draw(data, {curveType: "function",
							width: 567, height: 280,
							vAxis: {maxValue: 10}, pointSize:5
							}
					);
			
		}
		
		function drawGoalsScoredBodypart() {
			jq("#goalscored_bodypart").show();
			jq("#goalscored_zone").hide();
			jq("#goalscored_pitchview").hide();
			jq("#goalscored_overtime").hide();
			
			var tot_leftfoot=0; var tot_rightfoot=0; var tot_headed=0; var tot_others=0;
			
			if(typeof obj_goals_scored != 'undefined' && obj_goals_scored != null && obj_goals_scored != ''){
				for(b=0;b<obj_goals_scored.length;b++)
				{
					tot_leftfoot = tot_leftfoot + parseInt(obj_goals_scored[b]['bodypart']['leftfoot']);
					tot_rightfoot = tot_rightfoot + parseInt(obj_goals_scored[b]['bodypart']['rightfoot']);
					tot_headed = tot_headed + parseInt(obj_goals_scored[b]['bodypart']['head']);
					tot_others = tot_others + parseInt(obj_goals_scored[b]['bodypart']['other']);	
				}
			}
		  // Create and populate the data table.
		  var data = google.visualization.arrayToDataTable([		
			['Body part', 'Left foot', 'Right foot', 'Headed', 'Other'],
			['',  tot_leftfoot, tot_rightfoot, tot_headed, tot_others]
		  ]);
		
		  // Create and draw the visualization.
		  total			=	tot_leftfoot+tot_rightfoot+tot_headed+tot_others;
		  var min_val 	= 	(total > 5)		?1:0;
		  min_val		=	0;
		  var grid_val 	= 	(total >= 5)	?5:(total < 2)?2:total;
		    new google.visualization.BarChart(document.getElementById('the-graph-2a')).
			  draw(data,
				   {width:557, height:280,
					hAxis: {title: "Most used body part",format:'#',
					gridlines:{
						count:grid_val
					},
					viewWindowMode:'explicit',
			    	viewWindow:{
			    		min:min_val
			    	}},
					vAxis: {title: "Goals by"},
					legend: {position: 'top'}}
			  );		  
		
		}
		
		/** Overtime */
		function drawGoalsScoredOvertime(){
			
			var datas = eval(global_goal_scored_overtime); 
			
			jq("#goalscored_overtime").show();
			jq("#goalscored_bodypart").hide();
			jq("#goalscored_zone").hide();
			jq("#goalscored_pitchview").hide();
			
			var data = google.visualization.arrayToDataTable(datas);
	
			// Create and draw the visualization.
			new google.visualization.LineChart(document.getElementById('the-graph-2ot')).
				draw(data, {curveType: "function",
							width: 567, height: 280,
							vAxis: {maxValue: 10}, 
							pointSize:5,
							colors:['#F90', '#36C', '#DC3912', '#109618', '#909']
							}
					);
			
		}

var current_team	=	73;
var blocks_svg;
var hash	=	window.location.hash.split('#');

jq(function() {

	jq( "#slider-range" ).slider({
		range: true,
		min: 1,
		max: 14,
		values: [ 0, 14 ],
		slide: function( event, ui ) {
			//console.log(event);return false;
			if(ui.values[ 0 ] == ui.values[ 1 ] || ui.values[ 0 ] == no_of_match || ui.values[ 1 ] == 1)
			{
				e = event;
				if(e.stopPropagation)
		    		e.stopPropagation();
		  		if(e.preventDefault)
		    		e.preventDefault();
		    	e.cancelBubble = true;
		  		e.cancel = true;
		  		e.returnValue = false;
			}
		},
		change: function( event, ui ) {
			var appearance_count = Math.abs(ui.values[ 1 ] - ui.values[ 0 ]);
			global_tmp_status	=	1;
			jq( "#between-matches" ).val( ui.values[ 0 ] + " and " + (ui.values[ 1 ] - 1));
			getStatResults(ui);			 
		}
	});

		url		=	url		+	jq('#competition option:selected').text().toLowerCase().replace(/ /g, '-')	+ '|' + jq('#season option:selected').text().toLowerCase().replace(/ /g, '-') +	'#0#90#any#any#season#1';

		var team_type	=	jq("#team_type").val();
		if(team_type	==	"all")
			url	=	url		+	"#all-matches";
		else

	function resetHash()
	{
		if(hash.length == 1)
		{
			hash =	['', '','','','',	''];
			disableSearch	=	0;
			updateHash();
		}
		else
		{
			switch_hashes();
			disableSearch	=	0;
		}
	}
	
	function updateHash()
	{
		hash[1] 	=	jq('td.selected span.heading').html().toLowerCase().replace(/ /g,'-');
		hash[2] 	=	jq('#competition :selected').text().toLowerCase().replace(/ /g,'-');
		hash[3]		=	jq('#season :selected').text().toLowerCase().replace(/ /g,'-');
		hash[4]		=	jq('#season').val();
		hash[5]		=	jq('#team_type :selected').text().toLowerCase().replace(/ /g,'-');
		hash[6]		=	jq('#between-matches').val().replace(/ and /,'-');
		hash[7]		=	(jq('#statistics-graph .graph-with-tabs:visible a.selected').html() || '').toLowerCase().replace(/ /g,'-');
		window.location.hash	=	hash.join('#');
	}

function drawBlocks()
{
	//alert('in draw blocks fn '+no_of_match);
	if(no_of_match == 1)
	{
		jq('.info_div').show();
		jq('#date-slider, #statistics-options, #statistics-graph').hide();
	}
	else
	{
		jq('.info_div').hide();
		jq('#date-slider, #statistics-options, #statistics-graph').show();
	}
	
	jq( "#between-matches" ).val( jq( "#slider-range" ).slider( "values", 0 ) +" and " + (no_of_match - 1) );
		
	 var divWidth = jq('#slider-blocks').width();
     
	 //work out the width of blocks based on number of matches
                        var maxGames = no_of_match-1;
                        var bWidth = (divWidth/maxGames);
                        blocks_svg.clear();
                        for( var i = 0; i < maxGames; i++ )
                        {
                           setBlock(i,bWidth);
                        }
}

function setBlock(i,bWidth)
{
                    blocks_svg.setStart();
                          
                    var pos = i == 0 ? 0 : i*bWidth;
					var info	=	match_info[i].split('##');
                    if(info[0] ==  'draw')                	color	=	'90-#d69630-#f69c0f';//#CB962C
                    if(info[0] ==  'win')                	color	=	'90-#6ac72b-#70d230';//#8EC422
                    if(info[0] ==  'lose')                	color	=	'90-#c8332c-#ef423a';//#ED4139  
                    blocks_svg.rect( pos, 0, bWidth-2, 31, 3).attr({
                        'stroke-opacity' : 0,
                        'stroke-width' : 0,
                        fill : color,//'#F04038',
                        'fill-opacity' : 0.8
                    });

                    var st = blocks_svg.setFinish();
                    
                    var time = 0;
                    
                    st.hover(function(event){
                        this.attr({
                           'fill-opacity' : 0.5,
                           fill : color
                        });
                        
                        var x = event.pageX;
                        var y = jq(document).scrollTop();

                        //internet explorer fallback
                        if( x === undefined )
                        {
                            x = event.clientX;
                        }

                        //adjust position
                        x -= jq('#slider-blocks').offset().left;
                        x -= jq('#hoverbox').width()/2;

                        //if no space at top
                        if( y > 270 )
                            y = 32;
                        else
                            y = -158;

                        jq('#hoverbox').css({
                            top : y,
                            left : x
                        });
                        var info	=	match_info[i].split('##');
                        jq('#hoverbox-indicator')[0].className = info[0];
                        jq('#hoverbox-indicator span').html(info[0][0].toUpperCase());
                        jq('#hoverbox-teams p').eq(0).html(info[1]);
                        jq('#hoverbox-teams p').eq(1).html(info[2]);
                        jq('#hoverbox-teams span').eq(0).html(info[3]);
                        jq('#hoverbox-teams span').eq(1).html(info[4]);
                        jq('#hoverbox-date').html(info[5]);
                        jq('#hoverbox-matchlink').attr('href',info[6]);
                        jq('#hoverbox-bottom div').eq(0).html(player_info[i]);
                        if(info[0] ==  'draw')                	color	=	'90-#d69630-#f69c0f';//#CB962C
                    	if(info[0] ==  'win')                	color	=	'90-#6ac72b-#70d230';//#8EC422
                    	if(info[0] ==  'lose')                	color	=	'90-#c8332c-#ef423a';//#ED4139
                    	active_hover	=	i;  
                        this.attr({
                           'fill-opacity' : 0.5,
                           fill : color//'#D33232'
                        });
                        
                    }, function(){
                        this.attr({
                           'fill-opacity' : 0.8,
                           fill : color//'#F04038'
                        });
                    });
                    
                    st.attr({
                        cursor : 'pointer'
                    })
                    
                    st.click(function(e){
                       //go to match 
                       	if(e.stopPropagation)
		    				e.stopPropagation();
		  				if(e.preventDefault)
		    				e.preventDefault();
                    });
                }
				/* NEW CODE */
                
                jq('#slider-blocks').hover(function(){
                    jq('#hoverbox').animate({
                        opacity : 1
                    },150,function(){
                        jq('#hoverbox').css({
                            display : 'block'
                        });
                    })
                    
                },function(){
                    jq('#hoverbox').css({
                        display : 'none'
                    });
                });
                jq('.hoverclose').click(function(){
                    jq('#hoverbox').fadeOut(100);
                });
                /* End NEW CODE */
               
function drawDuelsWon(){
	var arg_duels_won = eval(global_duels_won);
	var tackle = arg_duels_won.tackle;
	var tackle_s = arg_duels_won.tackle_success;
	var tackle_f = arg_duels_won.tackle_fail;
	
	jq('#duels_won_tackle_title').html('Tackle - '+tackle_s+'/'+parseInt(tackle_s+tackle_f));
	jq('#duels_won_tackle').children('div.left-graph-desc').html(tackle+'% Successful');
	jq('#duels_won_tackle').children('div.right-graph-desc').html(Math.round(100-tackle)+'% Unsuccessful');
	jq('#duels_won_tackle').children('div.graph-box').children('div.left-item').css('width',tackle+'%');
	
	
	var foul = arg_duels_won.foul;
	var foul_s = arg_duels_won.foul_success;
	var foul_f = arg_duels_won.foul_fail;
	
	jq('#duels_won_foul_title').html('Fouls - '+foul_f+'/'+parseInt(foul_f+foul_s));
	jq('#duels_won_foul').children('div.left-graph-desc').html(Math.round(100-foul)+'% Suffered');
	jq('#duels_won_foul').children('div.right-graph-desc').html(foul+'% Committed');
	jq('#duels_won_foul').children('div.graph-box').children('div.left-item').css('width',Math.round(100-foul)+'%');
	
	
	var takeon = arg_duels_won.takeon;
	var takeon_s = arg_duels_won.takeon_success;
	var takeon_f = arg_duels_won.takeon_fail;
	
	jq('#duels_won_takeon_title').html('Take on - '+takeon_s+'/'+parseInt(takeon_s+takeon_f));
	jq('#duels_won_takeon').children('div.left-graph-desc').html(takeon+'% Successful');
	jq('#duels_won_takeon').children('div.right-graph-desc').html(Math.round(100-takeon)+'% Unsuccessful');
	jq('#duels_won_takeon').children('div.graph-box').children('div.left-item').css('width',takeon+'%');
	
	var headed_duel = arg_duels_won.headed_duel;
	var headed_duel_s = arg_duels_won.headed_duel_success;
	var headed_duel_f = arg_duels_won.headed_duel_fail;
	
	jq('#duels_won_headed_duel_title').html('Headed Duel - '+headed_duel_s+'/'+parseInt(headed_duel_s+headed_duel_f));
	jq('#duels_won_headed_duel').children('div.left-graph-desc').html(headed_duel+'% Successful');
	jq('#duels_won_headed_duel').children('div.right-graph-desc').html(Math.round(100-headed_duel)+'% Unsuccessful');
	jq('#duels_won_headed_duel').children('div.graph-box').children('div.left-item').css('width',headed_duel+'%');
	if(parseInt(tackle_s+tackle_f) == 0)
		jq('#duels_won_tackle div').eq(1).addClass('grey').children().addClass('grey');
	else
		jq('#duels_won_tackle div').eq(1).removeClass('grey').children().removeClass('grey');
	if(parseInt(headed_duel_s+headed_duel_f) == 0)
		jq('#duels_won_headed_duel div').eq(1).addClass('grey').children().addClass('grey');
	else
		jq('#duels_won_headed_duel div').eq(1).removeClass('grey').children().removeClass('grey');
	if(parseInt(takeon_s+takeon_f) == 0)
		jq('#duels_won_takeon div').eq(1).addClass('grey').children().addClass('grey');
	else
		jq('#duels_won_takeon div').eq(1).removeClass('grey').children().removeClass('grey');
	if(parseInt(foul_f+foul_s) == 0)
		jq('#duels_won_foul div').eq(1).addClass('grey').children().addClass('grey');
	else
		jq('#duels_won_foul div').eq(1).removeClass('grey').children().removeClass('grey');	
	
}

function drawDuelsWonOvertimeGraph(){
	var MARKER = '$^$';
	var datas = eval(global_duels_won_overtime); 
	var data = google.visualization.arrayToDataTable(datas);

	// Create and draw the visualization.
	new google.visualization.LineChart(document.getElementById('the-graph-10ot')).
		draw(data, {curveType: "function",
					width: 537, height: 280,
					vAxis: {maxValue: 10, viewWindow:{max:100, min:0}, viewWindowMode :'explicit', format: MARKER + '#'}, pointSize:5
					}
			);
		jq("text:contains('" + MARKER + "')").each(
					function(label, index) {
						//console.log(label + jq(this).text());
						val = jq(this).text().replace(MARKER, '');
						jq(this).text(val+'%');
				});	
}

function number_format (number, decimals, dec_point, thousands_sep) {
    number = (number + '').replace(/[^0-9+\-Ee.]/g, '');
    var n = !isFinite(+number) ? 0 : +number,
        prec = !isFinite(+decimals) ? 0 : Math.abs(decimals),
        sep = (typeof thousands_sep === 'undefined') ? ',' : thousands_sep,
        dec = (typeof dec_point === 'undefined') ? '.' : dec_point,
        s = '',
        toFixedFix = function (n, prec) {
            var k = Math.pow(10, prec);
            return '' + Math.round(n * k) / k;
        };
    // Fix for IE parseFloat(0.55).toFixed(0) = 0;
    s = (prec ? toFixedFix(n, prec) : '' + Math.round(n)).split('.');
    if (s[0].length > 3) {
        s[0] = s[0].replace(/\B(?=(?:\d{3})+(?!\d))/g, sep);
    }
    if ((s[1] || '').length < prec) {
        s[1] = s[1] || '';
        s[1] += new Array(prec - s[1].length + 1).join('0');
    }
    return s.join(dec);
} 

function switch_competition(feed_id)
{
	var cur_args	=	arguments;
	
	//Newly added for team type
	var team_type	=	jq("#team_type").val();
	
	jq.ajax({
				type: "GET",
				url: search_call_url+"stats_process.php?switch_id="+feed_id+"&team_type="+team_type,
				data: "rand="+Math.random(),
				dataType: "html",
				success: function(output){
					jq('#season').html(output);
					
					/** Newly modified for default selection 
					var sel_season = jq('#season').children('option:nth-child(2)').val();
					if(typeof sel_season != undefined){
						jq('#season').children('option:nth-child(2)').attr("selected", true);
						switch_season(sel_season)
					}
					* End */
					
					if(cur_args.length == 1){
						if(jq('#season')[0].children.length > 1)
						{
							jq('#season')[0].selectedIndex=1;
							switch_season(jq('#season').val());
						}
					}
					else{
						jq('#season').val(cur_args[1]);
						switch_season(cur_args[1],cur_args[2],cur_args[3],cur_args[4],cur_args[5]);
					}
				}
			});	
}
function switch_season(season_id)
{
	var cur_args	=	arguments;
	if(season_id == '') return;
	
	//Newly added for team type
	var team_type	=	jq("#team_type").val();
	
	jq.ajax({
				type: "GET",
				url: search_call_url+"stats_process.php?season_id="+season_id+"&team_id="+73+"&team_type="+team_type,
				data: "rand="+Math.random(),
				dataType: "json",
				success: function(output){
					new_total	=	parseInt(output[0]);
					
					/** Newly added for team type */
					if(output[1] == null) {
						jq('.info_div').show();
						jq('#date-slider, #statistics-options, #statistics-graph').hide();
						return;
					}
					/** End - team type */
					
					for(var x=0; x<output[1].length; x++ )
					match_info[x] = output[1][x];
					if(isNaN(new_total)) new_total=0;
					no_of_match	=	new_total+1;
					
					global_tmp_status	=	0;
					
					jq('#slider-range').slider( "option", "max", no_of_match );
					
					if(cur_args.length == 1)
							jq('#slider-range').slider( "option", "values", [0,no_of_match] );
					else
						{
							if(isNaN(cur_args[1])) cur_args[1] = 1;
							if(isNaN(cur_args[2])) cur_args[2] = no_of_match;
							jq('#slider-range').slider( "option", "values", [cur_args[1],cur_args[2]] );
						}	
					
					if(!global_tmp_status)
						getStatResults();
											
					drawBlocks();
					
					if(cur_args.length >1)
					 jq('#between-matches').val(cur_args[1]+' and '+(cur_args[2]-1));
										
					if(output[2].length)
					{
						for(z=0;z<output[2].length; z++)
						player_info[z]	=	' Performance score : '+output[2][z];
					}
					if(output[3].length)
					{
							var total_p	=	output[3].length;
							var html_p	=	jq('li.players-card').length;
							if(total_p < html_p)
							{
								for(i = total_p; i < html_p; i++)
								jq('li.players-card').eq(i).hide();
							}
							if(total_p > html_p)
							{
								for(i = html_p; i < total_p; i++)
								{
									if(jq('.slider-block:last').find('li').length%8 == 0)
									jq('#players-list').append(jq("<div/>").addClass('slider-block'));
									jq('.slider-block:last').append(jq('li.players-card').eq(0).clone());
								}
								
							}
							for(i = 0; i < total_p; i++)
							{
								jq('li.players-card').eq(i).show().attr('id', 'player_html_id_'+output[3][i].player_id).attr('class' , 'players-card '+output[3][i].position.substr(0,4));
								jq('li.players-card a').eq(i).attr('href', output[3][i].player_profile_url);
								jq('li.players-card img').eq(i).attr('src', search_call_url+'uploaded_icons/players/'+output[3][i].photo);
								if(output[3][i].name != null)
									jq('li.players-card span').eq(i*2).html(output[3][i].name.substr(0,14));
								jq('li.players-card span').eq(i*2+1).html(output[3][i].position);
								//jq('li.players-card span').eq(i*2+3).html(output[3][i].score).attr('id', 'player_score_id_'+output[3][i].player_id);
								//console.log(output[3][i].name);
							}
							jq('li.players-card:visible').each(function(index)
							{
								jq(this).css({'margin-right':'10px', 'margin-left':'0px'});
								if(index%8 == 0)
								jq(this).css({'margin-left':'27px'});
								if((index+1)%8 == 0)
								jq(this).css({'margin-right':'27px'});
								
							});
							var width	=	Math.ceil(jq('li.players-card:visible').length/8) * 940;
							jq('#players-list').css({'marginLeft':'0px', 'width':width+'px'});
					}
					if(cur_args.length > 1){
						/*jq("#"+cur_args[3]).bind('click',function(){
							if(cur_args[4] != ''){
								jq("#"+cur_args[4]).trigger('click');
							}
						});
						
						jq("#"+cur_args[3]).trigger('click');*/
						var found	=	'';
						jq('#statistics-options td span.heading').each(function(ind,ele){ 
							if(ele.innerHTML.toLowerCase().replace(/ /g,'-') == cur_args[3])
							{
								found = ele.parentNode.id;
								return true;
							}
							
						});
						if(found != '')
						{
							jq('#'+found).trigger('click');
							found	=	found.replace('-', '-graph-');
							jq('#'+found+' a').each(function(ind,ele)
							{ 
								if(ele.innerHTML.toLowerCase().replace(/ /g,'-') == cur_args[4])
								{
									jq(ele).trigger('click');
									return true;
								}
								
							});
						}
					}
					jq("img.lazy").show();
				}
			});
}

function showPlayers(type)
{
	if(type == 'all')
	{
		jq('.Goal').show();jq('.Defe').show();jq('.Midf').show();jq('.Forw').show();
	}
	if(type == 'goal')
	{
		jq('.Goal').show();jq('.Defe').hide();jq('.Midf').hide();jq('.Forw').hide();
	}
	if(type == 'defe')
	{
		jq('.Goal').hide();jq('.Defe').show();jq('.Midf').hide();jq('.Forw').hide();
	}
	if(type == 'midf')
	{
		jq('.Goal').hide();jq('.Defe').hide();jq('.Midf').show();jq('.Forw').hide();
	}
	if(type == 'forw')
	{
		jq('.Goal').hide();jq('.Defe').hide();jq('.Midf').hide();jq('.Forw').show();
	}
	jq('li.players-card:visible').each(function(index)
	{
		jq(this).css({'margin-right':'10px', 'margin-left':'0px'});
		if(index%8 == 0)
		jq(this).css({'margin-left':'27px'});
		if((index+1)%8 == 0)
		jq(this).css({'margin-right':'27px'});
		
	});
	var width	=	Math.ceil(jq('li.players-card:visible').length/8) * 940;
	jq('#players-list').css({'marginLeft':'0px', 'width':width+'px'});
}     

function limit_slider(min, max)
{
	if(jq( "#slider-range" ).slider( "values", 0 ) == min && jq( "#slider-range" ).slider( "values", 1 ) == max)
	return ;
	hs=jq('#slider-range').slider();
	hs.slider('option', 'values',[min, max]);
	hs.slider('option','change')
	       .call(hs,null,{ handle: jq('.ui-slider-handle', hs), values: [min, max] });
}
   </script>
   <script type="text/javascript">
    jq(document).ready(function(){
	
	var current_url 	= 	window.location.href;
	var shareid_index	=	-1; //current_url.indexOf("#");
	
	if(parseInt(shareid_index)>0 && parseInt(shareid_index)!=0){
		var share_id 	= 	current_url.substring(shareid_index+1,current_url.length);
		jq.ajax({
                type : "POST",
                url : search_call_url + "shared_stats_provider.php",
                data : "share_id="+share_id+"&rand="+Math.random(),
                dataType : "json",
                success : function(output) {
                	var result = eval(output);
                	if(result != null){
                		
                		jq("#competition").val(result['competition_id']);
                		
                		var limit_split	=	result['slider_limits'].split(",");
                		
                		if(result['team_type'] != undefined)
                			jq("#team_type").val(result['team_type']);
                		
                		switch_competition(result['competition_id'],result['season_id'],limit_split[0],limit_split[1],result['stats_type'],result['stats_sub_type']);						
						
					}
                }
     	});
	}
});

function switch_hashes()
{
  if(hash[1] == '') return null;
  jq('#competition').setSelect(hash[2]);
  jq("#team_type").setSelect(hash[5]);
  var limit =	hash[6].split('-');
  //console.log(hash);
  switch_competition(jq('#competition').val(), hash[4], limit[0], parseInt(limit[1])+1, hash[1], hash[7]);
}
